      <h3><span id="Articles_created.2Fexpanded_on_May_12"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Articles_created/expanded_on_May_12">Articles created/expanded on May 12</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Template_talk:Did_you_know&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Articles created/expanded on May 12">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Special_motion_to_strike">Special motion to strike</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FSpecial_motion_to_strike&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special_motion_to_strike&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Court_of_Appeals_for_the_Ninth_Circuit" title="United States Court of Appeals for the Ninth Circuit">Ninth Circuit</a> has held that a <b><a href="/wiki/Special_motion_to_strike" title="Special motion to strike">special motion to strike</a></b>, the <a href="/wiki/Motion" title="Motion">motion</a> allowed by the anti-<a href="/wiki/Strategic_lawsuit_against_public_participation" title="Strategic lawsuit against public participation">SLAPP</a> statute in <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a>, can be used in <a href="/wiki/Federal_judiciary_of_the_United_States" title="Federal judiciary of the United States">federal court</a> as well as state court? <small>Source: Batzel v. Smith, 333 F.3d 1018, 1025 (9th Cir. 2003). ("Because California law recognizes the protection of the anti-SLAPP statute as a substantive immunity from suit, this Court, sitting in diversity, will do so as well.")</small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that government-funded <a href="/wiki/Nonprofit_organization" title="Nonprofit organization">non-profits</a> are not subject to a <b><a href="/wiki/Special_motion_to_strike" title="Special motion to strike">special motion to strike</a></b>, and so are exempt from <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a>'s anti-<a href="/wiki/Strategic_lawsuit_against_public_participation" title="Strategic lawsuit against public participation">SLAPP</a> law? <small>Source: Cal. Code of Civil Procedure § 425.17 subd. (d) ("Any nonprofit organization that receives more than 50 percent of its annual revenues from federal, state, or local government grants, awards, programs, or reimbursements for services rendered.")</small></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li class="mw-empty-elt"></li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <p><small>Created by <a href="/wiki/User:Amitabho" title="User:Amitabho">Amitabho</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Amitabho" title="User talk:Amitabho">talk</a>). Self-nominated at 01:05, 15 May 2021 (UTC).</small> </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li>The article is long enough and new enough. It is written in an encyclopedic style with inline references. There are a few cases of bare URLs being used as references (ref 5, 8, and 23 in the current version); please express them as formatted citations. I think ref 23 should be treated carefully: this is a "newsroom alert" by a law firm, so it is written by a professional expert but it is effectively self-published. I think the text should attribute it as the analysis of one particular firm rather than stating it as fact.</li>
        </ul> 
        <dl>
         <dd>
          The copyvio detector finds a lot of text common between the article and existing sources, especially in the sections on Commercial speech and Exceptions, where you've reproduced some of the legal code. If we are dealing with legal text that is in the public domain, then it would be okay to reuse it: I don't know if that's the case with California State law as opposed to Federal law, so I welcome clarification on this. In the lead, the phrase "speech made in connection with an issue under consideration or review by a legislative, executive, or judicial proceeding, or any other official proceeding authorized by law" seems to be verbatim from an existing source, maybe itself drawing from the legal code. It needs to be rephrased unless the legal code itself is in the public domain, in which case the source needs to be cited. You've helpfully provided web links for most of the legal documents cited, and I have to assume good faith on the rest: if you provide web links for more of the citations, that's welcome but not mandatory.
         </dd> 
         <dd>
          I think the original hook is a bit hard to take in with its multiple clauses referring to three different courts, but ALT1 expresses an interesting and digestable fact. This fact is expressed in the article with a suitable inline source. A QPQ seems to be not necessary in this case as the nominator has not made 5 DYK noms. You've done good work creating an accessible overview of a piece of legislation and there are just small changes needed to get this to the required standard (fix citations and clarify the copyright status, or rephrase text where necessary). <a href="/wiki/File:Symbol_question.svg" class="image"><img alt="Symbol question.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/16px-Symbol_question.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/24px-Symbol_question.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/32px-Symbol_question.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="180" data-file-height="185"></a> <a href="/wiki/User:MartinPoulter" title="User:MartinPoulter">MartinPoulter</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:MartinPoulter" title="User talk:MartinPoulter">talk</a>) 14:04, 1 June 2021 (UTC) 
          <dl>
           <dd>
            Having looked up <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://leginfo.legislature.ca.gov/faces/home.xhtml">[12]</a> it seems that the legal code on that site is in the public domain, so there isn't a copyright issue, but I ask you to just make sure that every time public domain text is used there is a citation to attribute it: the Commercial speech/ Exemptions sections look okay in this regard, but there is also that "speech made in connection with..." part of the lead which needs citation or rewording. <a href="/wiki/User:MartinPoulter" title="User:MartinPoulter">MartinPoulter</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:MartinPoulter" title="User talk:MartinPoulter">talk</a>) 14:13, 1 June 2021 (UTC)
           </dd>
          </dl>
         </dd>
        </dl>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <h3><span id="Articles_created.2Fexpanded_on_May_13"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Articles_created/expanded_on_May_13">Articles created/expanded on May 13</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Template_talk:Did_you_know&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Articles created/expanded on May 13">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="On_China">On China</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FOn_China&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=On_China&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that <i><b><a href="/wiki/On_China" title="On China">On China</a></b></i> is a 2011 book made by <a href="/wiki/Henry_Kissinger" title="Henry Kissinger">Henry Kissinger</a> which provides authentic insights into the personalities of China's most infamous communist leaders <a href="/wiki/Mao_Zedong" title="Mao Zedong">Mao Zedong</a> and <a href="/wiki/Zhou_Enlai" title="Zhou Enlai">Zhou Enlai</a>?</li> 
       <li><b>ALT1:</b> ... that <i><b><a href="/wiki/On_China" title="On China">On China</a></b></i> is part of an effort to make sense of China's strategy in diplomacy and foreign policy over 3000 years and part an attempt to provide an authentic insight on Chinese Communist Party leaders? <small>Source:<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[1]</a></sup></small></li>
      </ul> 
      <p><small>Created/expanded by <a href="/wiki/User:Clancoo" title="User:Clancoo">Clancoo</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Clancoo" title="User talk:Clancoo">talk</a>). Self-nominated at 03:41, 24 May 2021 (UTC).</small> </p>

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Nurhajizah_Marpaung">Nurhajizah Marpaung</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FNurhajizah_Marpaung&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Nurhajizah_Marpaung&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that former <a href="/wiki/List_of_vice_governors_of_North_Sumatra" title="List of vice governors of North Sumatra">vice governor of North Sumatra</a> <b><a href="/wiki/Nurhajizah_Marpaung" title="Nurhajizah Marpaung">Nurhajizah Marpaung</a></b> was involved in a human rights violation trial during her service in the military? <small>Source: ref. #4 in the article</small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that a poll conducted at the end of <b><a href="/wiki/Nurhajizah_Marpaung" title="Nurhajizah Marpaung">Nurhajizah Marpaung</a></b><span class="nowrap">'s</span> term showed that only 12.4% of the respondents were satisfied with her performance as vice governor? <small>Source: ref. #26 in article</small></li> 
         <li><b>ALT2</b>:... that <b><a href="/wiki/Nurhajizah_Marpaung" title="Nurhajizah Marpaung">Nurhajizah Marpaung</a></b> was the first woman to serve as vice governor of North Sumatra? <small>"North Sumatra gets first female deputy governor." <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.thejakartapost.com/news/2017/03/09/north-sumatra-gets-first-female-deputy-governor.html">The Jakarta Post</a></small></li>

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Gallagh_Man">Gallagh Man</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FGallagh_Man&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Gallagh_Man&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 162px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Galagh_Man.jpg" class="image" title="Gallagh Man"><img alt="Gallagh Man" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Galagh_Man.jpg/162px-Galagh_Man.jpg" decoding="async" width="162" height="122" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Galagh_Man.jpg/243px-Galagh_Man.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Galagh_Man.jpg/324px-Galagh_Man.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4000" data-file-height="3000"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Gallagh Man
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that the Irish <a href="/wiki/Bog_body" title="Bog body">bog body</a> <b><a href="/wiki/Gallagh_Man" title="Gallagh Man">Gallagh Man</a></b> preserves the remains of a first century BC man, who was six-foot tall, around 25-year-old, dark haired man, and was either strangled during a <a href="/wiki/Human_sacrifice" title="Human sacrifice">ritual killing</a> or executed as a criminal? 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that ...? <small>Source: "You are strongly encouraged to quote the source text supporting each hook" (and [link] the source, or cite it briefly without using citation templates)</small></li>
        </ul></li>

      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><b>Review</b>. The article is 5x expanded. It is long enough, interesting to read and well cited. Earwig copyvio indicates copyvio is unlikely and repeats appear to be of book titles. QPQ is not required as this is the first nomination. Pic is fine, CC 2.0. The hook is inaccurate and needs to be altered. It says that he was ritually killed, whereas the article gives that as an option <i>or</i> put to death as a common criminal. The hook could be reworded to include both possibilities, the words ritual killing removed or other hooks offered. If adding new hooks ensure that those same words are used in the article and referenced at the end of that sentence. <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Desertarun&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Desertarun (page does not exist)">Desertarun</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Desertarun" title="User talk:Desertarun">talk</a>) 15:00, 27 May 2021 (UTC)</li>
        </ul>

         <dd>
          <ul>
           <li>Thank.           </ul>

           <dd>

            </ul> 
            <dl>
             <dd>
              <ul>
               <li>There is a character limit of 200 and this is 220, so a bit too long. I've added an Alt or you could reword. <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Desertarun&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Desertarun (page does not exist)">Desertarun</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Desertarun" title="User talk:Desertarun">talk</a>) 07:07, 5 June 2021 (UTC)</li>

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Juren">Juren</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FJuren&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Juren&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that <b><a href="/wiki/Juren" title="Juren">Juren</a></b> was a rank awarded in imperial China for those who passed the provincial level of the civil examination system? <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://doi.org/10.3982/ECTA13448">[14]</a> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that in 1630, less than 2.6% of 49,200 or so <i><b><a href="/wiki/Juren" title="Juren">juren</a></b></i> candidates was awarded that rank? <small>Source: <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AGF" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:AGF">WP:AGF</a>; someone with access should check ch. 3, "Circulation of Ming-Qing Elites" in <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.jstor.org/stable/j.ctt6wppq7">Elman 2013</a></small> 
          <ul>
           <li><b>ALT2</b>:... that ...? <small>Source: "You are strongly encouraged to quote the source text supporting each hook" (and [link] the source, or cite it briefly without using citation templates)</small></li>
          </ul></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul>

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sheikh_Jarrah_property_dispute">Sheikh Jarrah property dispute</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FSheikh_Jarrah_property_dispute&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Sheikh_Jarrah_property_dispute&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 171px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Sheikh_Jarrah_Demonstration_6_August_2010_3.JPG" class="image" title="Sheikh Jarrah solidarity demonstration"><img alt="Sheikh Jarrah solidarity demonstration" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Sheikh_Jarrah_Demonstration_6_August_2010_3.JPG/171px-Sheikh_Jarrah_Demonstration_6_August_2010_3.JPG" decoding="async" width="171" height="114" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Sheikh_Jarrah_Demonstration_6_August_2010_3.JPG/257px-Sheikh_Jarrah_Demonstration_6_August_2010_3.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Sheikh_Jarrah_Demonstration_6_August_2010_3.JPG/342px-Sheikh_Jarrah_Demonstration_6_August_2010_3.JPG 2x" data-file-width="3888" data-file-height="2592"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Sheikh Jarrah solidarity demonstration
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that the deputy mayor of Jerusalem explained that the <b><a href="/wiki/Sheikh_Jarrah_property_dispute" title="Sheikh Jarrah property dispute">Sheikh Jarrah eviction cases</a></b> are part of a municipal strategy to create “layers of Jews” throughout East Jerusalem? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.nytimes.com/2021/05/07/world/middleeast/evictions-jerusalem-israeli-palestinian-conflict-protest.html">Evictions in Jerusalem Become Focus of Israeli-Palestinian Conflict</a>, May 7, 2021: "But Mr. King, the deputy mayor, said “of course” they are part of a wider strategy of installing “layers of Jews” throughout East Jerusalem. That policy, Mr. King said, “is the way to secure the future of Jerusalem as a Jewish capital for the Jewish people.” “If we will not be in big numbers and if we will not be at the right places in strategic areas in East Jerusalem,” he added, then future peace negotiators “will try to divide Jerusalem and to give part of Jerusalem to our enemy.”"</small></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/The_Chariot_of_Israel:_Britain,_America_and_the_State_of_Israel" title="Template:Did you know nominations/The Chariot of Israel: Britain, America and the State of Israel">Template:Did you know nominations/The Chariot of Israel: Britain, America and the State of Israel</a></li>
        </ul>
       </dd>

           <li><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NPOV" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:NPOV">Neutral</a>: <img alt="Green tick" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Green_check.svg/13px-Green_check.svg.png" decoding="async" width="13" height="13" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Green_check.svg/20px-Green_check.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Green_check.svg/26px-Green_check.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="600"><span style="display:none">Y</span></li> 
           <li>Free of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Copyright_violations" title="Wikipedia:Copyright violations">copyright violations</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Plagiarism" title="Wikipedia:Plagiarism">plagiarism</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Close_paraphrasing" title="Wikipedia:Close paraphrasing">close paraphrasing</a>: <img alt="Green tick" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Green_check.svg/13px-Green_check.svg.png" decoding="async" width="13" height="13" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Green_check.svg/20px-Green_check.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Green_check.svg/26px-Green_check.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="600"><span style="display:none">Y</span></li>
          </ul> </td>
        </tr>
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <p><b>Hook eligibility:</b> </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Did_you_know#Cited_hook" title="Wikipedia:Did you know">Cited</a>: <img alt="Green tick" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Green_check.svg/13px-Green_check.svg.png" decoding="async" width="13" height="13" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Green_check.svg/20px-Green_check.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Green_check.svg/26px-Green_check.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="600"><span style="display:none">Y</span></li>

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Rosalie_Carey">Rosalie Carey</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FRosalie_Carey&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Rosalie_Carey&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 120px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Gg-tue-13-apr-2010-afternoon-investitures-auckland-rosalie-carey-2_(cropped).jpg" class="image" title="Rosalie Carey in 2010"><img alt="Rosalie Carey in 2010" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Gg-tue-13-apr-2010-afternoon-investitures-auckland-rosalie-carey-2_%28cropped%29.jpg/120px-Gg-tue-13-apr-2010-afternoon-investitures-auckland-rosalie-carey-2_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="120" height="163" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Gg-tue-13-apr-2010-afternoon-investitures-auckland-rosalie-carey-2_%28cropped%29.jpg/180px-Gg-tue-13-apr-2010-afternoon-investitures-auckland-rosalie-carey-2_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Gg-tue-13-apr-2010-afternoon-investitures-auckland-rosalie-carey-2_%28cropped%29.jpg/240px-Gg-tue-13-apr-2010-afternoon-investitures-auckland-rosalie-carey-2_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="992" data-file-height="1347"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Rosalie Carey in 2010
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that when playwright <b><a href="/wiki/Rosalie_Carey" title="Rosalie Carey">Rosalie Carey</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i> staged <i>Amy Robsart</i> in 1940 she used a suit worn by Sir <a href="/wiki/Henry_Irving" title="Henry Irving">Henry Irving</a> for the leading man? <small>Source: "the costume worn by Mr M. Burdis, who plays the part of “Tressilian,” is a suit originally worn by the famous English actor, Sir Henry Irving, in one of the many parts played by him in the plays of Shakespeare" (from a <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://paperspast.natlib.govt.nz/newspapers/WT19400518.2.99.8">contemporary newspaper review</a> of the play, written and performed in by Carey)</small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that when Patric and <b><a href="/wiki/Rosalie_Carey" title="Rosalie Carey">Rosalie Carey</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i> built the <a href="/wiki/Globe_Theatre,_Dunedin" title="Globe Theatre, Dunedin">Globe Theatre, Dunedin</a> in their house, it was the first purpose-built theatre for professional repertory in New Zealand? <small>Source: "Instrumental in developing and fostering New Zealand actors, directors and writers, the Globe was the first purpose-built theatre for professional repertory in the country." (From <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.odt.co.nz/news/dunedin/southern-honours-rosalie-louise-carey">Otago Daily Times</a>)</small></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/La_Bonne_Cuisine:_Four_Recipes_for_Voice_and_Piano" title="Template:Did you know nominations/La Bonne Cuisine: Four Recipes for Voice and Piano">La Bonne Cuisine</a></li>
        </ul>
       </dd>

Earwigs copyvio is showing some close paraphrasing <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://copyvios.toolforge.org/?lang=en&amp;project=wikipedia&amp;title=Rosalie_Carey">see here</a>. The hooks need adjusting, I've added a new one below, as I've now contributed to the nomination I'll ask for a new reviewer.</li>
      </ul>

      <h4><span id="Flightless_.28Record_Label.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Flightless_(Record_Label)">Flightless (Record Label)</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FFlightless_%28Record_Label%29&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li>

      </div> 
      <ul>

The nomination, by an editor new to DYK, was made on an expansion that began on May 16, when the article was 2022 prose characters, and the article is currently 9426 prose characters, only 684 prose characters short of 5x. We typically allow an IAR exception for new nominators if they're a little late (only three days in this case), and we typically allow any nominator a chance to make up the difference if they come up a little short in the expansion department, since many don't know how to count prose characters. What is more serious is that the article will need to be edited to deal with getting better sourcing and encyclopedic tone—both these issues will need to be addressed before the nomination can proceed, and the resulting article will need to be at least 10110 prose characters. Pinging <a href="/wiki/User:Rhododendrites" title="User:Rhododendrites">Rhododendrites</a> (given how close this was to a 5x expansion, the "X" was probably not appropriate) and <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Desertarun&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Desertarun (page does not exist)">Desertarun</a> (seven days is standard to allow for issues like this to be noted before rejecting a nomination). <a href="/wiki/User:BlueMoonset" title="User:BlueMoonset">BlueMoonset</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:BlueMoonset" title="User talk:BlueMoonset">talk</a>) 04:25, 28 May 2021 (UTC)</li>

                  No comments on your hook, and thanks for the offer, but - in defense of my rewriting <i>what was proposed</i> (my hook would again be different from all of these, but I try to help the nominator): the J. Kennedy fact is not <i>plot</i> in the sense we want to avoid as something fictional, but may be the common ground to connect to Halston. - Now, if he is famous and I'm the only one whom the name alone told zero, forget this&nbsp;;) - Halston - "its subject" - could have been a place, a ship, ... - a hook should not rely on people already knowing what it is. --<a href="/wiki/User:Gerda_Arendt" title="User:Gerda Arendt">Gerda Arendt</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Gerda_Arendt" title="User talk:Gerda Arendt">talk</a>) 07:59, 19 May 2021 (UTC) 
                  <dl>
                   <dd>
                    No, I got you. So, Halston is a famous fashion designer, very famous for the pillbox hat incident, but we can't assume anyone would know him. Nobody needs to know him to understand a hook about a movie. Because it shouldn't be about him. He's not the bold article.
                   </dd> 
                   <dd>
                    And I think this is an important thing that is ruled out by PLOT, so let me explain. My point was, your entire hook is a very long-winded way of describing him, not the movie - and whether he's "the American fashion designer" <i>or</i> "the American fashion designer who designed the iconic <a href="/wiki/Pillbox_hat" title="Pillbox hat">pillbox hat</a>" <i>or</i> "the American fashion designer who designed the iconic <a href="/wiki/Pillbox_hat" title="Pillbox hat">pillbox hat</a> that <a href="/wiki/Jacqueline_Kennedy" class="mw-redirect" title="Jacqueline Kennedy">Jacqueline Kennedy</a> wore" <i>or</i> "the American fashion designer who designed the iconic <a href="/wiki/Pillbox_hat" title="Pillbox hat">pillbox hat</a> that <a href="/wiki/Jacqueline_Kennedy" class="mw-redirect" title="Jacqueline Kennedy">Jacqueline Kennedy</a> wore to her husband's <a href="/wiki/John_F._Kennedy_1961_presidential_inauguration" class="mw-redirect" title="John F. Kennedy 1961 presidential inauguration">presidential inauguration</a>", it is just an ever-more wordy way of replacing his name. He could be a complete unknown and it would be the same point - say it was a fictional film with a brand new character nobody knows, we wouldn't say "X movie is about Y character", even if you spun it into "X movie is about the person who did Y with Z who did A". Either it's saying "film is about main character" in a far too convoluted way, or it is summarizing the PLOT (i.e. it's what the character does in the work - fiction or not, you will know the hook fact by merely watching the work, thus it doesn't have anything "real life" i.e. outside of the film content. The hat is in the movie, it is PLOT).
                   </dd> 
                   <dd>
                    Basically, we don't assume people know who the film is about, but it's not hooky to simply tell them who that is, no matter how many details of that person you give. Like, would you say "<i>Mission Impossible</i> is about an American spy who famously hangs from a rappel wire in an impossible mission he survived"? No. Nor would you say, if you want to challenge how I see PLOT applying, "that <i>Mission Impossible</i> stars the American actor known for his short stature, wonky smile, and Scientology". Why use such lengthy descriptors and avoid a name, why describe a person instead of say anything about the boldlinked movie? We can write plenty of interesting hooks about movies without ever needing to identify the subject, and simply "fashion designer" is an adequate descriptor of Halston, if he is mentioned, for those that don't know. <a href="/wiki/User:Kingsif" title="User:Kingsif">Kingsif</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Kingsif" title="User talk:Kingsif">talk</a>) 09:57, 19 May 2021 (UTC)
                   </dd> 
                   <dd>
                    You're right, <i>Halston</i> could be about anything, and while your point seems to be that we should just tell people what that is (and in a way that establishes the notability as if it was the opening sentence of his article), my point is that it doesn't matter at all whether people know what a movie is about or not. It's hooky to say "that <i>Jaws</i> deliberately avoided showing a shark, both to create suspense and because the production did not have a waterproof model", and not "<i>Jaws</i> is about three men on a small boat who are scared by a shark". A documentary example for perhaps better comparison: hooky is "that one of the interviewees describing violence towards trans women in <i>Paris is Burning</i> was killed in an incidence of this during production", and not "<i>Paris is Burning</i> is about the American drag queens and trans women from the New York ball scene". <a href="/wiki/User:Kingsif" title="User:Kingsif">Kingsif</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Kingsif" title="User talk:Kingsif">talk</a>) 10:06, 19 May 2021 (UTC)
                   </dd>
                  </dl>
                 </dd>
                </dl>
               </dd>
              </dl>
             </dd>
            </dl>
           </dd>
          </dl>
         </dd>
        </dl> 
        <ul>
         <li>And since I've added so much, I can do a review <i>not considering my proposed hooks</i>. The good: article new and long enough, written well enough, interesting and sourced. Second nom so no QPQ needed. Hooks are sourced inline (well, in footnote) and check out...</li> 
         <li><a href="/wiki/File:Symbol_possible_vote.svg" class="image"><img alt="Symbol possible vote.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Symbol_possible_vote.svg/16px-Symbol_possible_vote.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Symbol_possible_vote.svg/24px-Symbol_possible_vote.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Symbol_possible_vote.svg/32px-Symbol_possible_vote.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="180" data-file-height="185"></a> And the bad: but the article sections are all out of order and "Production notes" is non-standard ("Production", it should be). This should be easily solvable. Hooks ALT0 through ALT2 are a mix of Easter egg and PLOT violations, with some plain "so what?" I am concerned with potential copyvio and certain at least close paraphrasing <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://copyvios.toolforge.org/?lang=en&amp;project=wikipedia&amp;oldid=1023887641&amp;action=compare&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fthecreativeindependent.com%2Fpeople%2Ffilmmaker-frederic-tcheng-on-the-detective-work-of-making-documentary-films%2F">shown here</a> from throughout the first two paragraphs of the "Production notes", the close para <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://copyvios.toolforge.org/?lang=en&amp;project=wikipedia&amp;oldid=1023887641&amp;action=compare&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.vogue.com%2Farticle%2Fhalston-documentary-frederic-tcheng-1970">shown here</a>, and I'll note that the article uses quotations so lengthy that they are +20% of their original sources, a similar concern. I'd like to ask <span class="template-ping">@<a href="/wiki/User:Isaidnoway" title="User:Isaidnoway">Isaidnoway</a>:</span> about the close paraphrasing, and someone else can look at the hooks. <a href="/wiki/User:Kingsif" title="User:Kingsif">Kingsif</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Kingsif" title="User talk:Kingsif">talk</a>) 11:13, 19 May 2021 (UTC)</li>
        </ul> 
        <dl>
         <dd>
          <ul>
           <li>There is absolutely no copyvio. The short phrases in the production section are limited, minimal and clearly attributed to Frédéric Tcheng, the director of the film. The <i>Vogue</i> passages are direct quotes supported by a reliable souce. Per - <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:PARAPHRASE" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:PARAPHRASE">WP:PARAPHRASE</a> - <i>Limited close paraphrasing is appropriate within reason, as is quoting, so long as the material is clearly attributed in the text. Limited close paraphrasing is also appropriate if there are only a limited number of ways to say the same thing.</i> There are no <a href="/wiki/Easter_egg_(media)" title="Easter egg (media)">easter eggs</a> in any of my hooks, (a message, image, or feature hidden in a video game, film, or other, usually electronic, medium). My preferred hooks are the original one and ALT 2. If those are not acceptable, I'm fine with that. If another hook is developed and used, I'm fine with that. If the DYK is declined, I'm fine with that as well. This was my first attempt at a self-nomination, and I definitely learned something for any potential future noms.<a href="/wiki/User:Isaidnoway" title="User:Isaidnoway"><b style="font-family:Times New Roman; color:blue"> <i>Isaidnoway</i> </b></a><a href="/wiki/User_talk:Isaidnoway" title="User talk:Isaidnoway"><b style="font-family:Times New Roman; color:green"><i>(talk)</i></b></a> 14:01, 19 May 2021 (UTC)</li>
          </ul> 
          <dl>
           <dd>
            <ul>
             <li>You're wrong on both accounts, and I'll assume it's misunderstandings: linking to the film when you're referring to the person is an Easter egg, where DYK is the medium, and there are clear instances of whole fragments or sentences that are prose from the sources - not quotations - either directly lifted or only slightly rearranged. That needs fixing: above, I linked comparisons of source and article text, and the worst is even highlighted, so you can't credibly deny it. Hooks about works aren't always easy to write, but not mentioning the film when the article is the film isn't going to pass. I'm trying to give extensive feedback to be helpful to someone new to DYK, rather than just say "no", so assuming your last sentence isn't spitefully sarcastic, you're welcome. <a href="/wiki/User:Kingsif" title="User:Kingsif">Kingsif</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Kingsif" title="User talk:Kingsif">talk</a>) 14:34, 19 May 2021 (UTC)</li>
            </ul> 
            <dl>
             <dd>
              <ul>
               <li>No, there is not any misunderstandings, just disagreement. I linked to the most common definition of an easter egg in relation to the media (which I assumed we were talking about, and not the Easter Bunny) and most frequently seen in films, like <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.radiotimes.com/tv/sci-fi/best-movie-easter-eggs/">16 of the best movie Easter eggs</a>, surely you recognize that terms you've hijacked for use in the DYK medium, don't necessarily reflect the mainstream view. I just assumed you all were using the common definition incorrectly. My bad, now I know. And I also linked you to the relevant policy <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:PARAPHRASE" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:PARAPHRASE">WP:PARAPHRASE</a>. And the analysis of the text vs source, shows 69 out of 501 words in that particular section, and when you subtract commonly used words that can't be avoided like "a" "to" "the" "that", the number is even less. So it is limited, fair use and attributed to the person who said it. I will add to that section the publication that interviewed Frédéric Tcheng and the date of the source as well. Thanks for your feedback.<a href="/wiki/User:Isaidnoway" title="User:Isaidnoway"><b style="font-family:Times New Roman; color:blue"> <i>Isaidnoway</i> </b></a><a href="/wiki/User_talk:Isaidnoway" title="User talk:Isaidnoway"><b style="font-family:Times New Roman; color:green"><i>(talk)</i></b></a> 16:39, 19 May 2021 (UTC)</li>

      <h4><span id="English_Building.2C_University_of_Illinois_Urbana-Champaign"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="English_Building,_University_of_Illinois_Urbana-Champaign">English Building, University of Illinois Urbana-Champaign</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FEnglish_Building&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=English_Building%2C_University_of_Illinois_Urbana-Champaign&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that according to campus legend, the <b><a href="/wiki/English_Building,_University_of_Illinois_Urbana-Champaign" title="English Building, University of Illinois Urbana-Champaign">English Building</a></b> at the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Illinois_Urbana-Champaign" title="University of Illinois Urbana-Champaign">University of Illinois Urbana-Champaign</a> is haunted by the ghost of a female student who drowned in the building's pool? Students using the building have reported mysterious phenomena and the faint voice of a woman sounding from nowhere." Source:<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20151101105212/http://www.las.illinois.edu/alumni/magazine/articles/2014/english/">[20]</a></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li class="mw-empty-elt"></li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <p><small>Created by <a href="/wiki/User:Chevsapher" title="User:Chevsapher">Chevsapher</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Chevsapher" title="User talk:Chevsapher">talk</a>). Nominated by <a href="/wiki/User:JustinMal1" title="User:JustinMal1">JustinMal1</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:JustinMal1" title="User talk:JustinMal1">talk</a>) at 13:46, 17 May 2021 (UTC).</small> </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><a href="/wiki/File:Symbol_possible_vote.svg" class="image"><img alt="Symbol possible vote.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Symbol_possible_vote.svg/16px-Symbol_possible_vote.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Symbol_possible_vote.svg/24px-Symbol_possible_vote.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Symbol_possible_vote.svg/32px-Symbol_possible_vote.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="180" data-file-height="185"></a> Article new and long enough, generally well written but poorly sourced. I would go so far as to say <i>most</i> of the article is unsourced or the sources aren't clear. I also highly recommend moving the article to <a href="/wiki/English_Building,_University_of_Illinois_Urbana-Champaign" title="English Building, University of Illinois Urbana-Champaign">English Building, University of Illinois Urbana-Champaign</a>. Just about every university will have an "English building", and many of them will be officially called that, let alone all the buildings named after people called English, or representing England at various events. It needs the disambiguation unless you think it's undoubtedly the main thing in existence referred to as "English building" (the answer is no, it isn't). What sources are used appear to be almost entirely primary sources, not indicating that it has outside notability. I am also concerned that <a href="/wiki/User:Chevsapher" title="User:Chevsapher">Chevsapher</a> has undisclosed COI (editing behavior)? Similarly, I would like more information on the licenses for the images in the article. But you and <a href="/wiki/User:JustinMal1" title="User:JustinMal1">JustinMal1</a> still have a few more days to work on the article before it would even be too late to nominate for DYK, and I'd offer a grace period for improvements after that date (24th) too. <a href="/wiki/User:Kingsif" title="User:Kingsif">Kingsif</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Kingsif" title="User talk:Kingsif">talk</a>) 17:27, 21 May 2021 (UTC)</li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <dl>
         <dd>
          <dl>
           <dd>
            Thank you for the helpful feedback. To address your points: 
            <ul>
             <li>~95% of the article is sourced, and the few statements that are not sourced are common general knowledge. If I need to change the citation style, I am happy to do so.</li> 
             <li>I like the suggestion about creating disambiguation page, and I saw that <a href="/wiki/User:JustinMal1" title="User:JustinMal1">JustinMal1</a> just moved the article to the suggested namespace.</li> 
             <li>Concerning the potential COI, I am a student at the university, but I am not affiliated with the units that occupy the building. If this is still qualifiable as a COI, I will stop editing University of Illinois articles.</li> 
             <li>The images' origins and licenses are explained on their Wikimedia pages. The photos I personally uploaded are photos I took myself.</li> 
             <li>I tried to avoid primary sources, but I will agree that many of the secondary sources are internal to the university. To add more external sources, I would need to dig more into two main reasons why the building is externally relevant, which are (1) it was designed by the pre-eminent architectural firm of the Beaux-Arts era, and (2) it was the home of one of the most influential early home economics departments in the U.S., whose research helped drive the early-20th-century revolution in domestic efficiency. I would love to flesh out this article more fully, but unfortunately, my time is limited. I cannot yet commit to spending a few full days with a stack of books.</li>
            </ul>
           </dd> 
           <dd>
            <a href="/wiki/User:Chevsapher" title="User:Chevsapher">Chevsapher</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Chevsapher" title="User talk:Chevsapher">talk</a>) 17:51, 22 May 2021 (UTC)
           </dd>
          </dl>
         </dd>
        </dl>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <h3><span id="Articles_created.2Fexpanded_on_May_18"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Articles_created/expanded_on_May_18">Articles created/expanded on May 18</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Template_talk:Did_you_know&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Articles created/expanded on May 18">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="September_2019_events_in_the_U.S._repo_market">September 2019 events in the U.S. repo market</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FSeptember_2019_events_in_the_U.S._repo_market&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=September_2019_events_in_the_U.S._repo_market&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that on September 17, 2019, <a href="/wiki/Interest_rates" class="mw-redirect" title="Interest rates">interest rates</a> on <a href="/wiki/Overnight" title="Overnight">overnight</a> <a href="/wiki/Repurchase_agreements" class="mw-redirect" title="Repurchase agreements">repurchase agreements</a> (or "repos"), which are short term loans between financial institutions, experienced a <a href="/wiki/September_2019_events_in_the_U.S._repo_market" title="September 2019 events in the U.S. repo market"><b>sudden and unexpected spike</b></a>?</li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT</b>:... that on September 17, 2019, <a href="/wiki/Interest_rates" class="mw-redirect" title="Interest rates">interest rates</a> on <a href="/wiki/Repurchase_agreements" class="mw-redirect" title="Repurchase agreements">repos</a>, which are short term loans between financial institutions, experienced a <a href="/wiki/September_2019_events_in_the_U.S._repo_market" title="September 2019 events in the U.S. repo market"><b>sudden and unexpected spike</b></a>?</li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl>

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jim_Clendenen">Jim Clendenen</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FJim_Clendenen&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li>

       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that <b><a href="/wiki/Jim_Clendenen" title="Jim Clendenen">Jim Clendenen</a></b> went into winemaking instead of law school after staying in <a href="/wiki/Bordeaux_wine_regions" title="Bordeaux wine regions">Bordeaux</a>, <a href="/wiki/Champagne_wine_region" title="Champagne wine region">Champagne</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Burgundy" title="Burgundy">Burgundy</a> for six months? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.nytimes.com/2021/05/19/dining/jim-clendenen-dead.html"><i>The New York Times</i></a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.beaconjournal.com/story/news/2021/05/18/big-hearted-au-bon-climat-winemaker-jim-clendenen-dies-age-68/5132334001/"><i>Akron Beacon Journal</i></a></small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that <b><a href="/wiki/Jim_Clendenen" title="Jim Clendenen">Jim Clendenen</a></b> and his business partner picked grapes and handled all aspects of <a href="/wiki/Au_Bon_Climat" title="Au Bon Climat">Au Bon Climat</a> because they "had no money to hire any labor"? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.nytimes.com/2021/05/19/dining/jim-clendenen-dead.html"><i>The New York Times</i></a></small></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul>

      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FEnamorado_Por_Primera_Vez_and_List_of_Billboard_Latin_Pop_Airplay_number_ones_of_1997&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a> )</li>

      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( Article history links: <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Enamorado_Por_Primera_Vez&amp;action=history">Enamorado Por Primera Vez</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=List_of_Billboard_Latin_Pop_Airplay_number_ones_of_1997&amp;action=history">List of Billboard Latin Pop Airplay number ones of 1997</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that "<b><a href="/wiki/Enamorado_Por_Primera_Vez" title="Enamorado Por Primera Vez">Enamorado Por Primera Vez</a></b>" by <a href="/wiki/Enrique_Iglesias" title="Enrique Iglesias">Enrique Iglesias</a> was the longest-running <b><a href="/wiki/List_of_Billboard_Latin_Pop_Airplay_number_ones_of_1997" title="List of Billboard Latin Pop Airplay number ones of 1997">number one song of 1997</a></b> on the <i><a href="/wiki/Billboard_(magazine)" title="Billboard (magazine)">Billboard</a></i> <a href="/wiki/Latin_Pop_Airplay" title="Latin Pop Airplay">Latin Pop Airplay</a> chart with 11 weeks? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=0g0EAAAAMBAJ&amp;pg=PA54">https://books.google.com/books?id=0g0EAAAAMBAJ&amp;pg=PA54</a></small></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: pending</li> 
         <li><i>Comment</i>: Enamorado Por Primera Vez achieved GA status and List of Billboard Latin Pop Airplay number ones of 1997 was expanded 5 fivefold</li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl>

      <h4><span id="Ancient_Dreams_in_a_Modern_Land_.28song.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Ancient_Dreams_in_a_Modern_Land_(song)">Ancient Dreams in a Modern Land (song)</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FAncient_Dreams_in_a_Modern_Land_%28song%29&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Ancient_Dreams_in_a_Modern_Land_%28song%29&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that a critic said <a href="/wiki/Marina_Diamandis" title="Marina Diamandis">Marina</a>'s "<b><a href="/wiki/Ancient_Dreams_in_a_Modern_Land_(song)" title="Ancient Dreams in a Modern Land (song)">Ancient Dreams in a Modern Land</a></b>" may be her return to the "internet-influenced anthems that populated <a href="/wiki/Tumblr" title="Tumblr">Tumblr</a> for years"? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.stereogum.com/2148343/marina-ancient-dreams-in-a-modern-land/music/"><i>Stereogum</i>: "Before that, she released the less ambitious album <i>Froot</i>, where she veered away from the idiosyncratic, internet-influenced anthems that populated Tumblr for years. This new track out today, though, 'Ancient Dreams In A Modern Land,' could be her re-entry back to that world."</a></small></li>
      </ul>

       <dd>

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Filiberto_Avogadro_di_Collobiano">Filiberto Avogadro di Collobiano</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FFiliberto_Avogadro_di_Collobiano&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Filiberto_Avogadro_di_Collobiano&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 132px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Filiberto_Avogadro_di_Colobiano.jpg" class="image" title="Filiberto Avogadro di Collobiano"><img alt="Filiberto Avogadro di Collobiano" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Filiberto_Avogadro_di_Colobiano.jpg/132px-Filiberto_Avogadro_di_Colobiano.jpg" decoding="async" width="132" height="149" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Filiberto_Avogadro_di_Colobiano.jpg/198px-Filiberto_Avogadro_di_Colobiano.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Filiberto_Avogadro_di_Colobiano.jpg/264px-Filiberto_Avogadro_di_Colobiano.jpg 2x" data-file-width="467" data-file-height="528"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Filiberto Avogadro di Collobiano
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that while King <a href="/wiki/Charles_Albert_of_Sardinia" title="Charles Albert of Sardinia">Charles Albert</a> initially mistrusted <b><a href="/wiki/Filiberto_Avogadro_di_Collobiano" title="Filiberto Avogadro di Collobiano">Filiberto Avogadro di Collobiano</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i>, he eventually appointed him to his <a href="/wiki/Royal_court" title="Royal court">royal court</a>? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.treccani.it/enciclopedia/avogadro-di-collobiano-filiberto_(Dizionario-Biografico)">Treccani</a></small></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/Harry_Harper" title="Template:Did you know nominations/Harry Harper">Harry Harper</a></li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl>

      <h4><span id="Trial_of_Abdullah_.C3.96calan"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Trial_of_Abdullah_Öcalan">Trial of Abdullah Öcalan</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FTrial_of_Abdullah_%C3%96calan&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Trial_of_Abdullah_%C3%96calan&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that for the <b><a href="/wiki/Trial_of_Abdullah_%C3%96calan" title="Trial of Abdullah Öcalan">trial of Abdullah Öcalan</a></b> in 1999, a new courtroom was built on <a href="/wiki/%C4%B0mral%C4%B1" title="?mral?">Imral? island</a>? <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/330868.stm">A special courthouse is being constructed on the island prison for next month's trial</a> <small>Source: "You are strongly encouraged to quote the source text supporting each hook" (and [link] the source, or cite it briefly without using citation templates)</small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that during the preparation for the <b><a href="/wiki/Trial_of_Abdullah_%C3%96calan" title="Trial of Abdullah Öcalan">trial of Abdullah Öcalan</a></b> the lawyers Öcalan were granted access to the case file of several thousand pages but not provided with a copy of it? <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.ch/books?id=QaJH0_cFLbUC&amp;pg=PA130&amp;lpg=PA130&amp;dq=öcalans+lawyers+attacked+april+1999&amp;source=bl&amp;ots=qt_nIf4Vh-&amp;sig=ACfU3U0YgpaWaJgeb2KYWEl3L4Mt1eaTIg&amp;hl=en&amp;sa=X&amp;ved=2ahUKEwjpoPq9kc_wAhWqwAIHHWr9Ab8Q6AEwBXoECAYQAw#v=onepage&amp;q&amp;f=false/">the case concerning Öcalan ... amounted to 17,000 pages, Öcalans lawyers were granted access to it on 7 May, but the authorities did not supply them with a copy. (Öcalans lawyers had to use their own photocopier and it took them until the 15 may to cry the case file)</a> p.130 / <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.amnesty.org/download/Documents/148000/eur440401999en.pdf">His lawyers did not obtain a copy ... according to his lawyers some 15,000 pages. The presiding judge ... told the lawyers copying the case file you don't need to copy all of them, it's a shame to waste your money</a> p.13 see reference 17 on the same page for the judges statement <small>Source: "You are strongly encouraged to quote the source text supporting each hook" (and [link] the source, or cite it briefly without using citation templates)</small></li> 
         <li><b>ALT2</b>:... that the <b><a href="/wiki/Trial_of_Abdullah_%C3%96calan" title="Trial of Abdullah Öcalan">trial of Abdullah Öcalan</a></b> in 1999 was held on <a href="/wiki/%C4%B0mral%C4%B1" title="?mral?">Imral? island</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Sea_of_Marmara" title="Sea of Marmara">Sea of Marmara</a>, but heard by judges coming from the State Security Court in Ankara on mainland Turkey? / <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.hrw.org/legacy/backgrounder/eca/turkey/security.htm">Ocalan's trial is scheduled to begin before the Ankara State Security Court on May 31, and will take place on the island of Imrali.</a></li> 
         <li><b>ALT3</b>:... that for the <b><a href="/wiki/Trial_of_Abdullah_%C3%96calan" title="Trial of Abdullah Öcalan">trial of Abdullah Öcalan</a></b> in 1999 a new courthouse was constructed on <a href="/wiki/%C4%B0mral%C4%B1" title="?mral?">Imral? island</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Sea_of_Marmara" title="Sea of Marmara">Sea of Marmara</a> south of <a href="/wiki/Istanbul" title="Istanbul">Istanbul</a>, but the case was heard by Judges coming from a State Security Court in <a href="/wiki/Ankara" title="Ankara">Ankara</a>?/<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/1999/feb/20/kurds/">small windswept island in the Sea of Marmara, 35 miles south-west of Istanbul</a><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.hrw.org/legacy/backgrounder/eca/turkey/security.htm">/Ocalan's trial is scheduled to begin before the Ankara State Security Court on May 31, and will take place on the island of Imrali.</a> and <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/330868.stm">A special courthouse is being constructed on the island prison for next month's trial</a></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li class="mw-empty-elt"></li> 
         <li><i>Comment</i>: That Ankara is on "Mainland Turkey" is to denote that Ankara is not an Island, which might not be obvious to some of our English speaking readers.<a href="/wiki/User:Paradise_Chronicle" title="User:Paradise Chronicle">Paradise Chronicle</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Paradise_Chronicle" title="User talk:Paradise Chronicle">talk</a>) 23:27, 28 May 2021 (UTC)</li>
        </ul>
       </dd>

      <p><b>Overall</b>: <a href="/wiki/File:Symbol_question.svg" class="image"><img alt="Symbol question.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/16px-Symbol_question.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/24px-Symbol_question.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/32px-Symbol_question.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="180" data-file-height="185"></a> I don't see any issues, but I think it's possible to improve on the hooks. Let me think of a couple suggestions. (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Buidhe" title="User talk:Buidhe">t</a> · <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Buidhe" title="Special:Contributions/Buidhe">c</a>) <b><a href="/wiki/User:Buidhe" title="User:Buidhe"><span style="color: black">buidhe</span></a></b> 00:52, 1 June 2021 (UTC) </p> 
      <ul>
       <li>Issue with these hooks is that they seem to presume the reader knows who Ocalan is. Perhaps consider something along the lines of the following:</li> 
       <li><b>ALT4</b> ... that the 1999 <b><a href="/wiki/Trial_of_Abdullah_%C3%96calan" title="Trial of Abdullah Öcalan">trial of Abdullah Öcalan</a></b>, the leader of the militant <a href="/wiki/Kurdistan_Workers%27_Party" title="Kurdistan Workers' Party">Kurdistan Workers' Party</a>, was ruled to be unfair by the <a href="/wiki/European_Court_of_Human_Rights" title="European Court of Human Rights">European Court of Human Rights</a>?</li> 
       <li><b>ALT5</b> ... that Turkey built a courtroom on <a href="/wiki/%C4%B0mral%C4%B1" title="?mral?">Imral? island</a> for the 1999 <b><a href="/wiki/Trial_of_Abdullah_%C3%96calan" title="Trial of Abdullah Öcalan">trial of Abdullah Öcalan</a></b>, the leader of the militant <a href="/wiki/Kurdistan_Workers%27_Party" title="Kurdistan Workers' Party">Kurdistan Workers' Party</a>?</li>
      </ul> 
      <p>(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Buidhe" title="User talk:Buidhe">t</a> · <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Buidhe" title="Special:Contributions/Buidhe">c</a>) <b><a href="/wiki/User:Buidhe" title="User:Buidhe"><span style="color: black">buidhe</span></a></b> 01:56, 1 June 2021 (UTC) </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        I am still new in the DYK process. I have now just made my <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:Did_you_know_nominations/Presidential_Transition_of_John_F._Kennedy&amp;diff=prev&amp;oldid=1026311889&amp;diffmode=source">first review</a> with a ? at the end. I left the creator of the article to choose one of the hooks, though. I don't know yet if this is really also the choice of the reviewer. I have done another DYK also but this one did not end with a ? yet. In this DYK, I'd agree with both ALT4 or ALT5, you choose. There are enough sources for both of the hooks in the article.<a href="/wiki/User:Paradise_Chronicle" title="User:Paradise Chronicle">Paradise Chronicle</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Paradise_Chronicle" title="User talk:Paradise Chronicle">talk</a>) 15:13, 1 June 2021 (UTC)

         <dd>

      <h3><span id="Articles_created.2Fexpanded_on_May_21"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Articles_created/expanded_on_May_21">Articles created/expanded on May 21</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Template_talk:Did_you_know&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Articles created/expanded on May 21">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2011_cloudburst_in_Denmark">2011 cloudburst in Denmark</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2F2011_cloudburst_in_Denmark&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li>

      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FSydney_Morton&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a> )</li>

       <li>... that <b><a href="/wiki/Sydney_Morton" title="Sydney Morton">Sydney Morton</a></b><span class="nowrap">'s</span> paternal grandfather appeared in <i><b><a href="/wiki/Run,_Little_Chillun" title="Run, Little Chillun">Run, Little Chillun</a></b></i> <i>(poster pictured)</i> but the musical theater bug skipped a generation? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="https://www.broadway.com/videos/158246/broadwaycom-liveatfive-with-sydney-morton-of-shes-gotta-have-it/">https://www.broadway.com/videos/158246/broadwaycom-liveatfive-with-sydney-morton-of-shes-gotta-have-it/</a> Quote: "It skipped a generation". </small></li>

      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>

       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 140px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Equisetum_similkamense_Dawson_1890_Fig1_a-c.png" class="image" title="illustrations of Equisetum similkamense fossils"><img alt="illustrations of Equisetum similkamense fossils" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Equisetum_similkamense_Dawson_1890_Fig1_a-c.png/140px-Equisetum_similkamense_Dawson_1890_Fig1_a-c.png" decoding="async" width="140" height="140" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Equisetum_similkamense_Dawson_1890_Fig1_a-c.png/210px-Equisetum_similkamense_Dawson_1890_Fig1_a-c.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Equisetum_similkamense_Dawson_1890_Fig1_a-c.png/280px-Equisetum_similkamense_Dawson_1890_Fig1_a-c.png 2x" data-file-width="465" data-file-height="465"></a>

         <dd>
          <ul>
           <li>The thing is that I'd like to tie it to the MLB All-Star Game. While there is no direct link (I looked through <a href="/wiki/Arch_Ward" title="Arch Ward">Arch Ward</a>'s columns advocating for an ASG in 1932 and he never referenced Joss), there are enough columnists that have made the connection that it's not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:OR" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:OR">WP:OR</a>. I've found, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.google.com/books/edition/The_Day_All_the_Stars_Came_Out/mqPTDRT2v3UC?hl=en&amp;gbpv=1">this book</a>, <i>The Day The All-Stars Came Out: Major League Baseball's First All-Star Game, 1933</i>, which talks about the Joss game in the first chapter. There's also articles there that I hadn't clipped yet, like <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.newspapers.com/clip/78421006/all-star-game-has-wisconsin-roots/">"All-Star Game has Wisconsin roots"</a>, which says the ASG was "inspired" by the Joss benefit game.</li> 
           <li>So here's ALT2:</li>
          </ul>
         </dd>

I remember that campaign well. They called him "Jimmy who?" because most people had never heard of him outside of the US State of Georgia. Even Carter joked about himself as "Jimmy who?" He was popular enough to win the nomination for the Democratic candidate, and popular enough to win the election. His popularity as President took some hits because of national issues he had to deal with. But it was never an issue in the 1976 Presidential campaign. <a href="/wiki/User:Maile66" title="User:Maile66">— Maile </a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Maile66" title="User talk:Maile66">talk</a>) 18:05, 21 May 2021 (UTC)</li>

      <h3><span id="Articles_created.2Fexpanded_on_May_22"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Articles_created/expanded_on_May_22">Articles created/expanded on May 22</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Template_talk:Did_you_know&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Articles created/expanded on May 22">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <h4><span id="Ludwig_W.C3.BCllner"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Ludwig_Wüllner">Ludwig Wüllner</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FLudwig_W%C3%BCllner&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Ludwig_W%C3%BCllner&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 125px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Nicola_Perscheid_-_Ludwig_W%C3%BCllner_um_1910.jpg" class="image" title="Ludwig Wüllner c. 1910"><img alt="Ludwig Wüllner c. 1910" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Nicola_Perscheid_-_Ludwig_W%C3%BCllner_um_1910.jpg/125px-Nicola_Perscheid_-_Ludwig_W%C3%BCllner_um_1910.jpg" decoding="async" width="125" height="156" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Nicola_Perscheid_-_Ludwig_W%C3%BCllner_um_1910.jpg/188px-Nicola_Perscheid_-_Ludwig_W%C3%BCllner_um_1910.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Nicola_Perscheid_-_Ludwig_W%C3%BCllner_um_1910.jpg/250px-Nicola_Perscheid_-_Ludwig_W%C3%BCllner_um_1910.jpg 2x" data-file-width="263" data-file-height="328"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Ludwig Wüllner c. 1910
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that <b><a href="/wiki/Ludwig_W%C3%BCllner" title="Ludwig Wüllner">Ludwig Wüllner</a></b> sang in the U.S. premiere of Mahler's <i><a href="/wiki/Kindertotenlieder" title="Kindertotenlieder">Kindertotenlieder</a></i> in 1910, conducted by the composer? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.de/books?id=dsfq_5dFeL0C&amp;pg=5105">[21]</a> (next page)</small></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/Five_Brahms_Waltzes_in_the_Manner_of_Isadora_Duncan" title="Template:Did you know nominations/Five Brahms Waltzes in the Manner of Isadora Duncan">Five Brahms Waltzes in the Manner of Isadora Duncan</a></li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <p><small>Created by <a href="/wiki/User:LouisAlain" title="User:LouisAlain">LouisAlain</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:LouisAlain" title="User talk:LouisAlain">talk</a>) and <a href="/wiki/User:Gerda_Arendt" title="User:Gerda Arendt">Gerda Arendt</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Gerda_Arendt" title="User talk:Gerda Arendt">talk</a>). Nominated by <a href="/wiki/User:Gerda_Arendt" title="User:Gerda Arendt">Gerda Arendt</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Gerda_Arendt" title="User talk:Gerda Arendt">talk</a>) at 21:24, 29 May 2021 (UTC).</small> </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li>New enough (just barely), long enough. QPQ done. While Earwig picks up <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://mahlerfoundation.org/mahler/contemporaries/ludwig-wullner/">this</a> as almost identical to the German article, I find it more likely that <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://mahlerfoundation.org/you/copyright/">they were the ones stealing</a>. Slight neutrality issues ("impressive", "fascinating" shouldn't be stated in Wikipedia's voice). The "Roles" section is entirely unsourced. Caption for the grave picture should be translated, and I don't quite see the point of the ad. Thesis title is mixed German/English and not in the source cited. (Untranslating the English part probably fixes that, see <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.digitale-sammlungen.de/en/view/bsb11023765?page=1">the thesis</a>). I find it fascinating that he had a PhD and an abortive academic career before becoming a singer. But your hook works (may want to add "pictured"), and is within the rules. <a href="/wiki/File:Symbol_question.svg" class="image"><img alt="Symbol question.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/16px-Symbol_question.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/24px-Symbol_question.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/32px-Symbol_question.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="180" data-file-height="185"></a> as some points about the article should be improved (neutrality, unreferenced section). —<a href="/wiki/User:Kusma" title="User:Kusma">Kusma</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Kusma" title="User talk:Kusma">talk</a>) 23:22, 3 June 2021 (UTC)

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Black-legged_seriema">Black-legged seriema</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FBlack-legged_seriema&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Black-legged_seriema&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 152px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Black-legged_seriema_crop.jpg" class="image" title="Black-legged seriema"><img alt="Black-legged seriema" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Black-legged_seriema_crop.jpg/152px-Black-legged_seriema_crop.jpg" decoding="async" width="152" height="129" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Black-legged_seriema_crop.jpg/228px-Black-legged_seriema_crop.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Black-legged_seriema_crop.jpg/304px-Black-legged_seriema_crop.jpg 2x" data-file-width="457" data-file-height="387"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Black-legged seriema
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that the <a href="/wiki/Toba_people" title="Toba people">Toba people</a> use <a href="/wiki/Poultice" title="Poultice">poultices</a> made from the manure of the <b><a href="/wiki/Black-legged_seriema" title="Black-legged seriema">black-legged seriema</a></b> to treat boils and abscesses? <small>"The use of poultices has the greatest consensus for animal pharmacopoeia, as for example the use of preparations with hen eggs (Gallus gallus) for burns and the manure of Chunga burmeisteri for furuncles and abscesses" Source: Martínez, Gustavo J.; Barboza, Gloria E. (28 October 2010). "Natural pharmacopoeia used in traditional Toba medicine for the treatment of parasitosis and skin disorders (Central Chaco, Argentina)". Journal of Ethnopharmacology. 132 (1): 86–100.</small></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/Rashid_Mahdi" title="Template:Did you know nominations/Rashid Mahdi">Rashid Mahdi</a></li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl>

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="North_Shore_Central_School_District">North Shore Central School District</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>

      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that <a href="/wiki/Long_Island" title="Long Island">Long Island</a>'s <b><a href="/wiki/North_Shore_Central_School_District" title="North Shore Central School District">North Shore School District</a></b> enthusiastically benefited from taxes on the <a href="/wiki/Glenwood_Generating_Station" title="Glenwood Generating Station">Glenwood Generating Station</a>, with one official saying "we endure the smoke, let's have the gravy"?</li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <small>Source: "The Glenwood trustees believe, according to Anderson, that it would be smart for the districts to combine and build a joint high school while they are still able to enjoy the full advantage of the heavy taxes contributed by the Long Island Lighting Co., from its large power plants. The utilities company has its largest electric power plant and has recently completed a mammoth gas manufacturing plant in the Glenwood Landing section. 'We endure the smoke, let's have the gravy,' Anderson said." <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.proquest.com/hnpnewsday/docview/872309488">[22]</a></small>

      <h4><span id="Die_g.C3.BCldne_Sonne_voll_Freud_und_Wonne"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Die_güldne_Sonne_voll_Freud_und_Wonne">Die güldne Sonne voll Freud und Wonne</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FDie_g%C3%BCldne_Sonne_voll_Freud_und_Wonne&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Die_g%C3%BCldne_Sonne_voll_Freud_und_Wonne&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 111px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Geistliche-Andachten-1667.jpg" class="image" title="Title page of the 1667 collection containing the song"><img alt="Title page of the 1667 collection containing the song" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/Geistliche-Andachten-1667.jpg/111px-Geistliche-Andachten-1667.jpg" decoding="async" width="111" height="176" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/Geistliche-Andachten-1667.jpg/167px-Geistliche-Andachten-1667.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/Geistliche-Andachten-1667.jpg/222px-Geistliche-Andachten-1667.jpg 2x" data-file-width="504" data-file-height="800"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Title page of the 1667 collection containing the song
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that in the morning song "<b><a href="/wiki/Die_g%C3%BCldne_Sonne_voll_Freud_und_Wonne" title="Die güldne Sonne voll Freud und Wonne">Die güldne Sonne voll Freud und Wonne</a></b>", <a href="/wiki/Paul_Gerhardt" title="Paul Gerhardt">the poet</a> found a new <a href="/wiki/Metre_(poetry)" title="Metre (poetry)">metre</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Johann_Georg_Ebeling" title="Johann Georg Ebeling">the composer</a> a new melody, to reflect getting up? <small>Source: several</small></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/Portrait_of_a_Woman_with_Mask" title="Template:Did you know nominations/Portrait of a Woman with Mask">Portrait of a Woman with Mask</a></li> 
         <li><i>Comment</i>: The sentence from the title page of the collection in which it is printed would be too long for DYK. Here for illustration purposes, - I guess it won't be taken anyway. "getting up" (or "rising"?) is meant in a broad sense: in the morning, from distress, perhaps even even from the dead. Help with wording welcome.</li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl>

      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FPortrait_of_a_Woman_with_Mask&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li>
